## Page 3

<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.46pt;color:#000000">仅供非商业用途或交流学习使用</span>

<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:11.82pt;color:#000000">内容简介</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.64pt;color:#000000">技术畅销书作者撰写，掌握高并发与</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.55pt;color:#000000">网络编程基石技术：</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.91pt;color:#000000">NIO</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.75pt;color:#000000">与</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.66pt;color:#000000">Socket</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.12pt;color:#000000"> 。</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.52pt;color:#000000">细</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.54pt;color:#000000">化到特性级别，涵盖缰；中区、通道、选择</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.82pt;color:#000000">器以及基于</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.58pt;color:#000000">Socket</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.40pt;color:#000000"> 的</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.73pt;color:#000000">TCP/IP</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.40pt;color:#000000">和</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.51pt;color:#000000">UDP</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.52pt;color:#000000">编</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.39pt;color:#000000">程</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.78pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.35pt;color:#000000">本书共</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.47pt;color:#000000">6</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.43pt;color:#000000">章，具体内窑如下</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.97pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.40pt;color:#000000">第</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.05pt;color:#000000">1</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.65pt;color:#000000"> 章讲解了</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.81pt;color:#000000">NIO</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.21pt;color:#000000"> 中的缰；中区，包括</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.51pt;color:#000000">核心</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.31pt;color:#000000">API</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.92pt;color:#000000"> 的使用。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.27pt;color:#000000">第</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.32pt;color:#000000">2</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.47pt;color:#000000">章讲解了</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.61pt;color:#000000">NIO</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.27pt;color:#000000"> 中的</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.64pt;color:#000000">Channel~i</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.30pt;color:#000000">董</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.51pt;color:#000000">类的继承关系、核心接口的作用，着重介</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.16pt;color:#000000">绍</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.02pt;color:#000000">FileChannel</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.33pt;color:#000000">类的使用</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.78pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.27pt;color:#000000">第</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.32pt;color:#000000">3</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.45pt;color:#000000">章涵盖利用</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.75pt;color:#000000">Ne</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.32pt;color:#000000">two</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.97pt;color:#000000"> 「</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.72pt;color:#000000">klnte</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.16pt;color:#000000"> 「</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.13pt;color:#000000">face</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.27pt;color:#000000">类</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.63pt;color:#000000">藏得网络接</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.40pt;color:#000000">口信</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.95pt;color:#000000">息方法、</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.24pt;color:#000000">lnetAdd</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.05pt;color:#000000"> 「</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.41pt;color:#000000">ess</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.40pt;color:#000000">和</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.43pt;color:#000000">lnte</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.36pt;color:#000000"> 「</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.36pt;color:#000000">faceAdd</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.16pt;color:#000000"> 「</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.22pt;color:#000000">ess</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.39pt;color:#000000">类的常见</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.16pt;color:#000000">A</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.43pt;color:#000000">PI</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.78pt;color:#000000"> 。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.02pt;color:#000000">第</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.27pt;color:#000000">4</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.13pt;color:#000000">章讲解使用</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.98pt;color:#000000">Java</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.16pt;color:#000000">语言实现</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.05pt;color:#000000">Socket</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.70pt;color:#000000">通信，基于</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.73pt;color:#000000">TCP/IP</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.27pt;color:#000000">和</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.89pt;color:#000000">U</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.23pt;color:#000000"> DP</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.68pt;color:#000000">协议进行实</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.39pt;color:#000000">现</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.21pt;color:#000000">。将</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.54pt;color:#000000">相关类的全部</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.37pt;color:#000000">API</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.50pt;color:#000000">进行了介绍</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:3.38pt;color:#000000">3</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.39pt;color:#000000"> 学</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.40pt;color:#000000">习后阅读相关的网络框架的源代码、</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.41pt;color:#000000">Java</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.30pt;color:#000000">高性能后台处理才不会迷茫</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.90pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.27pt;color:#000000">第</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.17pt;color:#000000">5</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.53pt;color:#000000">童讲解了</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.66pt;color:#000000">NIO</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.60pt;color:#000000">技术中非常重要的</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.15pt;color:#000000">Selecto</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.77pt;color:#000000">「选择器技术，</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.20pt;color:#000000">“多</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.61pt;color:#000000">路复用”精髓</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.77pt;color:#000000">在此体现，本章也是大幅提升程序运行效</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.06pt;color:#000000">率之关键。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.40pt;color:#000000">第</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.41pt;color:#000000">6</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.51pt;color:#000000">章</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.24pt;color:#000000">i</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.54pt;color:#000000">井解异步</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.94pt;color:#000000">1/0</span><span style="font-family:'Helvetica';font-size:9.50pt;color:#000000"> ( </span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.90pt;color:#000000">AIO</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.51pt;color:#000000"> ），旨在</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.81pt;color:#000000">NIO</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.77pt;color:#000000">的基础上实现异步执行、回调处理等</span>

## Page 6

## Page 8

<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.83pt;color:#000000">仅供非商业用途或交流学习使用</span>

<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:11.37pt;color:#000000">为什么要写这本书</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.22pt;color:#000000">早在几</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.37pt;color:#000000">年前，笔者就曾想</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.99pt;color:#000000">过</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.30pt;color:#000000">整理一</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.22pt;color:#000000">份</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.28pt;color:#000000">基于</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.24pt;color:#000000">Java</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.22pt;color:#000000"> 语</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.99pt;color:#000000">言</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.64pt;color:#000000">的</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.15pt;color:#000000">NIO</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.88pt;color:#000000"> 与</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.25pt;color:#000000">Socket</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.36pt;color:#000000"> 相关的稿件，因为</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.33pt;color:#000000">市面</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.38pt;color:#000000">上大部分的</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.15pt;color:#000000">Java</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.88pt;color:#000000"> 书</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.33pt;color:#000000">籍都是</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.40pt;color:#000000">以</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.99pt;color:#000000">l</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.11pt;color:#000000"> 章</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.99pt;color:#000000">或</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.44pt;color:#000000">2</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.39pt;color:#000000"> 章的篇幅介绍</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.89pt;color:#000000">N</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.60pt;color:#000000">IO</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.88pt;color:#000000"> 与</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.25pt;color:#000000">Socket</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.41pt;color:#000000"> 技术，并没有完整地</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.29pt;color:#000000">覆盖该技术</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.31pt;color:#000000">的知识点，而限于当时的时间及精力，一直没有如愿</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.39pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.55pt;color:#000000">机会终于来了，公司</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.59pt;color:#000000">要搭建基</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.62pt;color:#000000">础构架知识体系，我负责公司该技术方向的培训，这</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.47pt;color:#000000">重燃</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.05pt;color:#000000">了我对</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.05pt;color:#000000">NIO</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.87pt;color:#000000"> 和</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.16pt;color:#000000">Socket</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.18pt;color:#000000"> 技术的热情</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.31pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.05pt;color:#000000">在学习</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.11pt;color:#000000">Java</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.19pt;color:#000000"> 技术的过程中，当学习了</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.11pt;color:#000000">Java</span><span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:9.80pt;color:#000000"> SE/Java </span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.03pt;color:#000000">EE</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000"> 之</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.41pt;color:#000000">后想探索更深层次的技术，如大数据</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.99pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.41pt;color:#000000">分布式和高并发类等，可能会遇到针对</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.20pt;color:#000000">NIO</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.19pt;color:#000000"> 、</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.25pt;color:#000000">Socket</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.42pt;color:#000000">的学习，但</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.25pt;color:#000000">NIO</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> 和</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.34pt;color:#000000">Socket</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.53pt;color:#000000"> 技术的学习并不像</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.34pt;color:#000000">JDBC</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.43pt;color:#000000"> 一样简单，学习</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.30pt;color:#000000">NIO</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> 和</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.19pt;color:#000000">S</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.23pt;color:#000000"> ocket</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.39pt;color:#000000"> 时可能</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.35pt;color:#000000">要</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.50pt;color:#000000">遇到很</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.29pt;color:#000000">多的</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.35pt;color:#000000">问题</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.46pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.57pt;color:#000000">为了在该技术领域有更高的追求，我将</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.25pt;color:#000000">NIO</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> 和</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.34pt;color:#000000">Socket</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.50pt;color:#000000"> 的技术点以教案的</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.39pt;color:#000000">方式进行了</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.23pt;color:#000000">整</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.47pt;color:#000000">理，并在公司中与同事</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.35pt;color:#000000">一</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.50pt;color:#000000">起进行学习和交流，同事的反响非常热烈</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.65pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.46pt;color:#000000">若干年</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.35pt;color:#000000">前</span>

<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.49pt;color:#000000">本书介绍</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.20pt;color:#000000">NIO</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> 和</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.34pt;color:#000000">Socket</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.12pt;color:#000000"> 开</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.56pt;color:#000000">发中最值得关注</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.18pt;color:#000000">的内</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.56pt;color:#000000">容，并给出个人的一些想法和</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.23pt;color:#000000">见</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.46pt;color:#000000">解，希</span>

<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:11.26pt;color:#000000">本书特色</span>

<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.25pt;color:#000000">识点，使读者看到代码及运行结果后就可以知道此项目要解决的是什么问题</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.50pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.22pt;color:#000000">这类似于网络</span>

<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.23pt;color:#000000">第</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.53pt;color:#000000">2</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.46pt;color:#000000"> 章介绍</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.25pt;color:#000000">NIO</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.46pt;color:#000000"> 技术中的</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.51pt;color:#000000">Channel</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.20pt;color:#000000"> （通道）类的继承关系</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.06pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.56pt;color:#000000">核心接口的作用，并重点介</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">绍</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.84pt;color:#000000">Fi</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.38pt;color:#000000"> l</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.69pt;color:#000000">eChanne</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.38pt;color:#000000"> l</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.45pt;color:#000000"> 类的使用，以增加读者对</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.20pt;color:#000000">NIO</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.40pt;color:#000000"> 操作</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.84pt;color:#000000">File</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.42pt;color:#000000"> 类的熟悉度</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.65pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.11pt;color:#000000">第</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.11pt;color:#000000">3</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.52pt;color:#000000"> 章介绍如何使用</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.89pt;color:#000000">N</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.08pt;color:#000000">etworklnterface</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.58pt;color:#000000"> 类获得网络接口的信息，包括</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.02pt;color:#000000">IP</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.39pt;color:#000000"> 地址</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.99pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">子网掩</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.38pt;color:#000000">码等，还会介绍</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.19pt;color:#000000">I</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.38pt;color:#000000">netAddre</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.48pt;color:#000000">ss</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.88pt;color:#000000"> 和</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.83pt;color:#000000">Interfac</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.94pt;color:#000000">巳</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.37pt;color:#000000">Address</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.39pt;color:#000000"> 类的常见</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.81pt;color:#000000">API</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.39pt;color:#000000"> 。</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.42pt;color:#000000">如果进行</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.19pt;color:#000000">Java</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.37pt;color:#000000"> 开发，且基于</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.31pt;color:#000000">Socket</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.45pt;color:#000000"> 技术，那么这章可以给你</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.23pt;color:#000000">需</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.40pt;color:#000000">要的信息</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.46pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.11pt;color:#000000">第</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.60pt;color:#000000">4</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.51pt;color:#000000"> 章介绍如何使用</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.19pt;color:#000000">Java</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.33pt;color:#000000"> 语</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.11pt;color:#000000">言</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.33pt;color:#000000">实现</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.28pt;color:#000000">Socket</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.99pt;color:#000000"> 通</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.11pt;color:#000000">信</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.39pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.28pt;color:#000000">Socket</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.51pt;color:#000000"> 通信是基于</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.55pt;color:#000000">TCP/IP</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.88pt;color:#000000"> 和</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.53pt;color:#000000">UDP</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.99pt;color:#000000"> 实</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.61pt;color:#000000">现的</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.58pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.91pt;color:#000000">另外，将介绍</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.22pt;color:#000000">ServerSocket</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.99pt;color:#000000"> 、</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.25pt;color:#000000">Socket</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.99pt;color:#000000"> 、</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.46pt;color:#000000">DatagramSocket</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.88pt;color:#000000"> 和</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.44pt;color:#000000">DatagramPacket</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:10.00pt;color:#000000"> 类的全部</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.70pt;color:#000000">API</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.39pt;color:#000000"> 。</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.28pt;color:#000000">只有熟练掌握</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.28pt;color:#000000">Socket</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.32pt;color:#000000"> 技术后，在阅读相关网络框架的源代码时才不会迷茫</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.58pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.69pt;color:#000000">也就是说，</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.33pt;color:#000000">如果读者想要进行</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.24pt;color:#000000">Java</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.31pt;color:#000000"> 高性能后台处理，那么必须要学习</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.25pt;color:#000000">Socket</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.27pt;color:#000000"> ，并且它是进行细化学习的</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.47pt;color:#000000">基</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.24pt;color:#000000">础</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.54pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">第</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.02pt;color:#000000">5</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.20pt;color:#000000"> 章介绍</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.10pt;color:#000000">NIO</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.30pt;color:#000000"> 技术中最重要的</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.19pt;color:#000000">Se</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.68pt;color:#000000">lector</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.79pt;color:#000000"> （选择器）技术</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.31pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.05pt;color:#000000">NIO</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.33pt;color:#000000"> 技术的核心一一</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.20pt;color:#000000">多路复</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.58pt;color:#000000">用就是在此章体现的</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.54pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.58pt;color:#000000">学习这章内容需要有</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.42pt;color:#000000">Socket</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.88pt;color:#000000"> 的</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.59pt;color:#000000">编程基础，这就是为什么在前面用两</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.36pt;color:#000000">章</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.63pt;color:#000000">篇幅来介绍</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.32pt;color:#000000">Java</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000"> 的</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.45pt;color:#000000">Socket</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.59pt;color:#000000"> 编程的原因</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.54pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.62pt;color:#000000">同步非阻</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.24pt;color:#000000">塞</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.71pt;color:#000000">可以大幅度提升程序运行的效率，就在</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.23pt;color:#000000">此</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.40pt;color:#000000">章体会一</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.35pt;color:#000000">下吧</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.65pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.23pt;color:#000000">第</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.36pt;color:#000000">6</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.61pt;color:#000000"> 章介绍</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.20pt;color:#000000">AIO</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.65pt;color:#000000"> 。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.15pt;color:#000000">AIO</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.72pt;color:#000000"> 是异步</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.36pt;color:#000000">IO,</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.25pt;color:#000000">NIO</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.72pt;color:#000000"> 是非阻</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.35pt;color:#000000">塞</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.69pt;color:#000000">IO</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.65pt;color:#000000"> 。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.15pt;color:#000000">AIO</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.35pt;color:#000000"> 在</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.25pt;color:#000000">NIO</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.75pt;color:#000000"> 的基础上实现了异</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.41pt;color:#000000">步执行、回调处理等高级功能，可以在不同的场景使用</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.10pt;color:#000000">AIO</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.99pt;color:#000000"> 或</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.15pt;color:#000000">NIO</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.22pt;color:#000000"> ，可以说</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.15pt;color:#000000">NIO</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.76pt;color:#000000"> 和</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.05pt;color:#000000">AIO</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.11pt;color:#000000"> 是</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.40pt;color:#000000">Java</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.60pt;color:#000000"> 高级程序员</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.44pt;color:#000000">、架构</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">师</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.63pt;color:#000000">等必须要</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.36pt;color:#000000">掌</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.66pt;color:#000000">握的技术</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.61pt;color:#000000">。</span>

<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:16.78pt;color:#000000">缓冲区的使用</span>

<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.05pt;color:#000000">学习</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.15pt;color:#000000">NIO</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.36pt;color:#000000"> 能更加接近架构级的技术体系，对未来的职业发展有非常好的促进作用</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.39pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.51pt;color:#000000">当你看到以上这段文字的时候，笔者要恭喜你，因为你正在往</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.24pt;color:#000000">Java</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.37pt;color:#000000"> 高性能</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.99pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.70pt;color:#000000">高并发、</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.46pt;color:#000000">高吞吐量技术的道路上迈进，也就代表着未来是有可能将自己的职业规划定位在</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.24pt;color:#000000">Java</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.28pt;color:#000000"> 高级</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.67pt;color:#000000">程序员、</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.28pt;color:#000000">Java</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.37pt;color:#000000"> 资深工程师，以及技术经理</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.55pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.37pt;color:#000000">技术总监或首席技术官</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.78pt;color:#000000">（</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.53pt;color:#000000">CTO</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.15pt;color:#000000"> ）这类职位上</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.39pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.22pt;color:#000000">这</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.55pt;color:#000000">些职位对</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.36pt;color:#000000">Java</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.42pt;color:#000000"> 技术的</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.12pt;color:#000000">掌</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.42pt;color:#000000">握是有</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.23pt;color:#000000">一</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.59pt;color:#000000">定要求和标准的，至少笔者认为要将自己对技术的关注点</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.22pt;color:#000000">从</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.91pt;color:#000000">SSH,</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.53pt;color:#000000">SSM</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.43pt;color:#000000"> 分离出去，落脚在多线程、并发处理</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.99pt;color:#000000">、</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.15pt;color:#000000">NIO</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.11pt;color:#000000"> 及</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.28pt;color:#000000">Socket</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.41pt;color:#000000"> 技术上，因为这些技术</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.27pt;color:#000000">是开发</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.15pt;color:#000000">Java</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.38pt;color:#000000"> 高性能服务器必须要掌握的，甚至有些第</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.98pt;color:#000000">三</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.38pt;color:#000000">方的优秀框架也在使用这些技术</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.31pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.49pt;color:#000000">先不说自己开发框架，即使想要读懂第</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.23pt;color:#000000">三</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">方框架的源代码，也要</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">掌</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.49pt;color:#000000">握上面提到的多线程</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.84pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.23pt;color:#000000">并</span>

<span style="font-family:'Helvetica';font-size:9.40pt;color:#000000">( 1 </span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.90pt;color:#000000">）多线程</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.56pt;color:#000000">可以这样说，高性能的解决方案一定离不开多线程，它可以使</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.06pt;color:#000000">l</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.35pt;color:#000000"> 个</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.54pt;color:#000000">CPU</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.49pt;color:#000000"> 几乎在同</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.23pt;color:#000000">一</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">时</span>

<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.61pt;color:#000000">让软件运行更流畅，处理的数据更多，以提升使用软件时的用户体验</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.39pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.11pt;color:#000000">在</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.19pt;color:#000000">Java</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.30pt;color:#000000"> 中，使用</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.53pt;color:#000000">Thread</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.62pt;color:#000000"> 类来实现多线程功能的处理</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.46pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.61pt;color:#000000">在学习多线程时＼要注意同步与异步的区别，也就是</span>
